The Municipal Chamber of Commerce Boy Scout Group Holds a Ceremony Today

Completion Ceremony of the Cenotaph for Four Martyrs 120

Change of Reception Location

Various Sectors Sent Eulogies

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce Boy Scout Group will hold a completion ceremony for the cenotaph of four martyrs, Luo Yunxiang, Mao Weixiang, Ying Wenda, and Bao Zhengwu, at 10:00 am today in the Shanghai Cemetery in Jiangwan. Various sectors were invited in advance to participate and share in the grand event. At the same time, a special issue on the completion of the cenotaph for the four martyrs was edited and distributed to various sectors at the cemetery. It was reported that the group originally planned to set up a reception area on Baoshan Road, but now it has been changed to board the train at the former Songhu Station inside the North Station due to the narrow space there. It was also reported that various sectors deeply mourned the sacrifice of the four martyrs for the country and sent eulogies, including from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Yang Hu, Ye Mojun, Ye Jiaxing, Shen Zechun, Wu Yunqi, the Municipal North Middle School, the Sugar Industry Association, and many others. It was reported that the reception train was also changed to depart from the North Station at 8:10 am today.

The original inscription of the cenotaph for the four martyrs is as follows: "When the Northeast was lost, our group felt the urgency of the day of national decline and remembered our responsibility. We worked hard to prepare, and on the night of January 28, the Japanese led dozens of aircraft and more than 10,000 marines to attack the prosperous Zhabei of our city. The citizens were slaughtered, their houses turned to ashes, the soldiers struggled in the hail of bullets, and the women and children groaned in the broken walls and wells. Suffering such devastation, the whole country was indignant. At that time, comrades raised their arms in response, and the refugee relief team, the frontline transport team, the rear service team, and the fireline stretcher team were immediately established. The next day, a collective meeting was held, and more than a hundred people decided to sacrifice their occupations, property, families, and lives to be loyal to the country and wrote oaths in blood. At that time, senior member Luo Yunxiang served as the leader of the seventh group of the rescue team, leading intermediate members Ying Wenda, Mao Zhengxiang, and Bao Zhengwu to rush to the war zone to rescue the wounded soldiers and civilians, saving more than a hundred people. Alas, who would have thought that after departing on the morning of January 31, they would not return for a long time. The refugees reported that they had been captured. Under public indignation, they were rescued in all directions. The enemy, fearing justice, pretended to promise to investigate and release them, but secretly falsely accused them of being spies and killed them. Alas, the martyrs' ambitions were not fulfilled, and their loyal bones were destroyed. Their noble spirit will last forever, and their heroic souls will not perish. We mourn the loss of our good friends as national heroes and have become forever separated. We encourage our comrades to continue their legacy and swear to avenge the family feud. Recalling the meaning of diligently serving the country until death, there should be sacrifices and worship for thousands of years. Therefore, together with the Chinese Red Cross Society, we built a cenotaph for the four martyrs in the Shanghai Cemetery in Jiangwan, this city, to promote their loyalty and bravery and to serve as an example. This is the inscription."

The Five British Banks Earned More Than 100 Million Last Year 124

According to the New Voice News Agency, most industries in this port were not prosperous last year, resulting in the bankruptcy of nearly a thousand companies. However, in the banking industry, although several small banks also experienced liquidation storms, most of them achieved considerable profits. In the depression of all industries, the banking industry alone is better, which is a畸形phenomenon. As for the detailed figures of the profits of official and commercial banks last year, they have been seen in various newspapers. The business performance of the five major British banks that hold power in China last year is explored below. According to the investigation, there are five British banks in China: Standard Chartered, Mercantile, HSBC, Oriental, and Chartered, all of which have very strong capital and are also very powerful in the financial industry. In 1934, the total net profit of the five banks was 8,821,000 pounds, equivalent to more than 120 million yuan in national currency, an increase of 442,000 pounds compared with 8,379,000 pounds the previous year, an increase of about 5% or more. It is said that most of the income of the banks is from buying and selling customs duties and securities transactions, and the profits from lending and discounting are very small, which is due to the low interest rates last year.

Case of the Chairman and Directors of the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange Being Accused 125

Plaintiff Recently Purchased Shares, Defendants Reject Right to Inquire

The Procedural Part Was Concluded Yesterday and Awaits Sentencing

Regarding the Chairman of the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange, Zhang Weiru, and the standing directors of the exchange, Yin Yunsheng and Shen Changgeng, due to their joint handling of the exchange's business in a manner that allegedly failed to gain the trust of shareholder Kuang Yefu from Guangdong, Kuang sent a letter of inquiry. Zhang and the others responded by stating that Kuang was a new shareholder and had no right to inquire about past matters, rejecting his inquiry. However, Kuang not only refused to relinquish his shareholder rights or remain silent but took further action, collecting evidence and filing a criminal self-accusation with the First Special District Court against Zhang, Yin, and Shen, requesting that the defendants be punished for collusion for personal gain, breach of trust, and embezzlement. The major

allegations of malfeasance

include five items: (1) Allegedly using the guise of the chairman's entertainment expenses to embezzle 36,000 yuan. The explanation states that in the nineteenth year, in addition to the monthly entertainment expenses of 500 yuan, the chairman allegedly deceived a small number of directors into resolving to add a huge sum of 36,000 yuan to the operating expenses as entertainment expenses. Since the entertainment expenses already had a fixed amount, how could additional expenses be added? The defendants had no choice but to create a guise to make up for the waste and deficits, which was actually a disguised form of embezzlement, without any doubt. (2) Embezzling 10,000 yuan donated for the construction of the Central Party Headquarters. In the twentieth year, 10,000 yuan was paid from the operating expenses as a donation for the

Central Party Headquarters

construction fee. In reality, the Central Party Headquarters did not receive this sum, and it was embezzled and divided among the defendants without any concealment. (3) Pledging the exchange's inventory of valuable securities for a mortgage of 120,000 yuan and privately misappropriating it. In July of the twentieth year, Zhang Weiru stole the receipt for the 250,000 yuan of post-reorganization treasury bonds held by the exchange in the custody of the Bank of Communications and used it to obtain a mortgage of 120,000 yuan from the Yichang Qianzhuang for private use. After the September 18th Incident, he tried to fabricate expenses and redeem it. (4) Embezzling 170,000 yuan in checks from the Four Ming Bank. In the second half of the twentieth year, the defendants took away from the exchange

Four Ming Bank

two checks, one for 120,000 yuan and one for 50,000 yuan, and their purpose was never clarified. It must have been jointly divided among the three, otherwise, there would be no reason for such a large sum to be ignored by each other. (5) Falsely claiming to have paid 170,000 yuan for the construction of the new exchange site. Earlier this year, the construction of the current new building was contracted through bidding by the Chen Yongxing Construction Company, and the payments made successively all had official receipts from the construction company. However, the 170,000 yuan paid in September of the twentieth year did not obtain an official receipt from the construction company at the time, colluding to embezzle, with clear signs. In summary, the above five items total an embezzlement of 500,600 yuan. This is only what the plaintiff knows;

how much more

is unknown is still uncertain. Therefore, the plaintiff requests that the defendants be arrested and severely punished, and also requests a civil lawsuit, asking the court to order the defendants to jointly return the embezzled 500,600 yuan in full to protect shareholder rights, etc. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Jiang Shuzi of the First Special Court opened a court session for interrogation. Defendant Zhang Weiru claimed to be on official business in Beijing, and only Yin Yunsheng and Shen Changgeng appeared in court. Judge Jiang immediately questioned the plaintiff, Kuang Yefu, about the intention of the lawsuit. According to his statement, he has five shares in the Chinese Merchants Securities Exchange, which were purchased in December of last year. Because he has discovered that the defendants have engaged in

collusion for illicit purposes

and collusive malfeasance, for the benefit of the entire company, he is filing a complaint. At this point, the defendants' lawyers, Wu Linkun, Wang Fuchang, Qin Liankui, Zhang Shizhao, and Chen Ying, raised the issue of the right to sue, requesting that the plaintiff's self-accusation be rejected. Judge Jiang also felt that whether the self-accusation could be filed in this case was indeed a question of procedure. Therefore, he decided to temporarily postpone the discussion of the facts of the case and ordered the lawyers of both parties to begin debating on the procedural point first in order to decide. Thus, the plaintiff's lawyer, Wang Jian, first stated the

reasons for the self-accusation,

then cited the legal basis, and finally cited the clauses of the agreement established by the recovery of the concession's legal rights and the establishment of the Chinese court, saying that in this case, the defendants did not need to follow the example of ordinary reporting of criminal offenders and could file a self-accusation according to the fifth clause of the agreement, etc. Subsequently, the lawyers defending the three defendants successively refuted, saying that although the plaintiff's self-accusation was based on the agreement, it should still be bound by the Criminal Procedure Law and that only

those who are directly harmed

can file a self-accusation. Now, the content of the plaintiff's complaint is all about the events of the nineteenth and twentieth years, and his shares were only purchased in December of the twenty-third year, so he is not directly harmed. Moreover, he only has five shares, which is not enough to qualify as a shareholder representative. The old company has long been dissolved, and the current new company only started in April of last year and was registered by the ministry. Even if the plaintiff wants to claim rights, he can only trace back to the date of registration. If he insists on inheriting his dividends, he should first file a lawsuit in the civil court to confirm his shareholder rights. Now he is directly filing a criminal lawsuit, which is illegal and should be rejected, etc. The court then announced that the debate on the procedural part was concluded and would be sentenced on the afternoon of the 19th.

(1) Those who fail to sweep the road after being urged by the government will be fined. The above is an excerpt from Article 42 of the Violation of Police Regulations Law. Violators will be fined up to 5 yuan. (1) Those who dry or boil all kinds of items that generate foul smells in densely populated areas without heeding the prohibition will be fined. The above is an excerpt from Article 46 of the Violation of Police Regulations Law. Violators will be detained for up to 15 days or fined up to 15 yuan. (1) Those who mix substances harmful to health in food and drink to seek improper profits will be fined. Article 47 of the Violation of Police Regulations Law. International Trade Bureau Releases Last Year's Consumption of Tobacco and Alcohol 127

Two Items Imported for 37 Million

With Tobacco Leaves Accounting for the Largest Figure

The International Trade Bureau released yesterday morning the import statistics of tobacco and alcohol consumption for last year. From January to December last year, tobacco imports totaled 33,399,227 yuan, an increase of more than 4 million compared to the total of 29,643,711 yuan in the previous year. According to the investigation, the reason is that after cigarettes started offering gifts, the consumption increased greatly, and the import of tobacco leaves flowed in continuously. The total number of tobacco leaves imported last year reached more than 15,750,000 customs gold units. The import quantity of alcohol was 3,243,451 yuan, with beer accounting for the largest figure, totaling 345,479 yuan, and Japanese sake accounting for the least, totaling 35,000 yuan. The total consumption of tobacco and alcohol totals 37,233,678 yuan.

Where Did the Hand Grenade Come From? A Child Was Killed in an Explosion 129

A Child Was Running with a Grenade

The Grenade Exploded After Falling to the Ground

At around 3:00 PM the day before yesterday, near the intersection of Qiqihar Road and Kunming Road in Hexingfang Lane, a child was running with a hand grenade of unknown origin. Due to carelessness, he slipped and fell to the ground, causing the grenade to fall to the ground as well. It exploded immediately with a loud bang. The child was seriously injured in the head and abdomen by the grenade, with blood and flesh flying everywhere, a tragic scene. Wang Laowu, a blind man who was watching the lane in Hexingfang, immediately reported it to the Chinese police stationed nearby, who forwarded the report to the Lin Road Police Station, ordering detectives to investigate. The child was taken to the hospital, but he died soon after due to his serious injuries. The body was sent to the autopsy office on Philien Road. After investigation, the deceased was identified as Ni A'kun, 12 years old, from Jiangyin, living at No. 21 Xinglong Street, Zhabei. His father, Ni Linsheng, is a peddler. However, the origin of the grenade is still unknown. Yesterday morning, the First Special District Court appointed prosecutor Song Genshan, forensic doctor Zhang Yan, and clerk Wang Zuyi to the scene to examine the body. According to Wang Laowu, 42 years old, from Yangzhou, who was watching the lane in Hexingfang, at around 3:00 PM yesterday afternoon, he saw the child coming from the south with a grenade in his hand, resembling a flashlight, about four inches long, running very fast. Then he saw him suddenly slip and fall, and the grenade exploded. So he reported to the police, etc. According to the statement of the deceased's father, Ni Linsheng, yesterday his son went out to buy things and did not have a grenade. He requested justice, etc. After obtaining the statement, Mr. Song instructed that the deceased, Ni A'kun, male, was indeed killed by a hand grenade before his death. The body was handed over to the father, Ni Linsheng, to take back for burial after signing a statement.

Robbers in the Industry Bureau Iron Factory Case Handed Over to the Public Security Bureau 130

Because the Pistol Was Lost by the Public Security Bureau

The Robbery Part of the Case Has Been Sentenced by the Court Yesterday

On the 1st of this month, at 1:55 PM, when the Iron Factory Department of the Industry Bureau Works Department at No. 630 Maohai Road was about to issue wages and year-end bonuses, several robbers armed with weapons broke into the accounting room and robbed 20,714 yuan in cash before fleeing. The factory watchman, Indian policeman Jishanxin, and Chinese detective Zhang Youming, along with Chinese policeman No. 377, captured Zhou A'gen, a Liyang native, on the spot, along with 18,709 yuan of the stolen money. They also shot and injured Chen Xiaowuzi, an accomplice, who died from a fatal wound. They seized a pistol and twelve bullets. Subsequently, Chinese Detective Chief Shang Wu continued to capture accomplices Liu Xiaowuzi from Yancheng and Wang A'fu from Zhenjiang, as well as suspects Wang Zhenrong from Yangzhou and Chen Guangyi, at No. 55 Huasheng Road and No. 5 in the Zhengxin Hotel at No. 66 on the same road in the French Concession. They seized two pistols and nineteen bullets (one of which was lost by the Public Security Bureau) and brought them to the Huishan Police Station. They were sent to the First Special District Court for interrogation. The details have been published in this newspaper. Wang Zhenrong and Chen Guangyi were found to be unrelated by the police and were requested to be released. The request was approved. The missing stolen money of 2,005 yuan was also recovered in full. Yesterday morning, Judge Jiang Shuzi found that one of the three pistols, an Astra pistol, was lost by the Fifth District Public Security Bureau during the January 28th Incident. The Municipal Public Security Bureau sent personnel to take the three defendants and the pistol for interrogation to find out how they obtained the pistol. The police stated their agreement. When questioned, the defendants' statements were the same as before. According to the statement of the lead detective Gao Wansheng, he requested that they be transferred for investigation and then sent back. Judge Jiang sentenced Zhou A'gen to eight years of imprisonment, Liu Xiaowuzi to nine years, and Wang A'fu to ten years and six months. The number of days of detention before the final judgment was set at two days to offset one day of imprisonment. The guns and ammunition were confiscated. Zhou A'gen and the other three, along with the Astra pistol, ten bullets, and one clip, were handed over to the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Murder and Robbery Sentenced to Life Imprisonment 131

Li Heshang, a local from Liujiazhai, Yangjing, Pudong, 27 years old this year, and his mistress, Li Yushi, a Suzhou woman (25 years old this year), were both housekeepers and amahs for Westerners at No. 247, Lane 261, Baisai Zhong Road in the French Concession. Li had a friend from the same village named Jin Kui, who was scheduled to get married in the near future. Because he lacked funds to make clothes, he discussed with Li and asked Li for help. At around 4:00 PM on the 9th of last month, Jin Kui held a hemp rope and Li held a pistol. They went to the Dahua Coal Ball Distribution Office at No. 3 Shanzhong Road to rob and obtained 12 jiao in small foreign currency before fleeing. Li rode away on a bicycle, heading west on Haige Road. At that time, the victim Xu Guochang followed behind. Li fled to the intersection of Fukaishan Road, where Xu reported to the Vietnamese police at No. 192, who caught up and pursued him. At the intersection of Baisai Zhong Road, the Vietnamese police at No. 434 also helped to pursue him. Li opened fire to resist arrest, killing the Vietnamese police officer at No. 192. At the same time, Li's right leg was also injured by the police's gunfire. He fled back to his employer's house, changed his clothes, lay on the bed, and handed the pistol to his mistress, Li Yushi, and his companion, Sun Linwen (28 years old) from Changshu, to hide. At that time, Li's employer, a Westerner, returned home. Li lied that he was injured by stray bullets in the encounter between the police and the robbers on the road and asked the owner to send him to the hospital for treatment. The Westerner reported the information to the police, who sent detective Zhou Buguang to investigate and solved the case, seizing the pistol and the coat worn by Li (with bullet holes) and the bicycle. Li, his mistress Yushi, and Sun Linwen were taken to the police station. The next day, they were sent to the Second Special Court for trial and detention. The details have been published in previous reports. After the police concluded their investigation, they charged Li with robbery resulting in death and violation of the regulations on the prohibition of military firearms under the Criminal Law, and charged Li Yushi and Sun Linwen with concealment of evidence. The case has been repeatedly studied by Judge Zhang Chaohai and was scheduled for sentencing. Yesterday, the sentencing date arrived. At 10:00 AM, Judge Zhang arrived at the first criminal court and ordered the defendants to be brought to the court. Li Heshang was sentenced to nine years of imprisonment for carrying a weapon and colluding in robbery, two years of imprisonment for possessing military firearms, and life imprisonment for killing with the intention of escaping punishment, with deprivation of public rights for life. Li Yushi and Sun Linwen were each sentenced to four months of imprisonment for helping to conceal evidence, with a two-year suspension.

Citizens Should Pay Attention to Preventing Rabies 135

The report from the Public Health Department of the Public Works Bureau states that the general public pays little attention to the prevention of rabies, which is a matter of great concern. Although heavy doses were used for those who were injected last year, the effect was not satisfactory. Those seeking treatment often disappeared before completing the injection process. These people are mostly laborers, and although they are told the importance of completing the injections, they are difficult to persuade.

The number of rabid dogs found last year has increased significantly. The general public rarely complies with the practice of putting muzzles on dogs, and taking dogs to the countryside risks infection. If this habit is not changed, rabies cannot be prevented. Even cats can be infected with this disease, and the danger is even greater at that time.

Even if the injection is completed after a person is poisoned, it cannot be determined that the disease will not develop. Currently, there is no other way to save lives except for injections. Therefore, the most important thing is prevention, to prevent infection.

Unfortunately, even the educated class does not know how easily dogs can be infected with this disease. Even when a dog is infected, its owner often denies it absolutely, because if their beloved dog is proven to be rabid, the owner's reputation and status will be lost.

Last year, the Health Department purchased injection raw materials from the Pasteur Institute in Paris because of their stronger potency. Now, it has reprinted a pamphlet on rabies to awaken the public's attention. The Health Department believes that the three municipal districts should jointly formulate measures to capture and eliminate all dogs without muzzles. For the sake of society, it is better to eliminate cats and dogs than to play with human lives. Therefore, sentimentality should be abandoned and reason should be followed.

Recent News from Hongqiao Sanatorium 136

The Hongqiao Sanatorium in western Shanghai, founded by Dr. Ding Fubao, a respected elder in the medical community, was completed last summer. It is beautifully decorated and well-equipped, with various electrotherapy machines, X-ray machines, cold air equipment, anesthesia rooms, delivery rooms, sterilization rooms, chemical laboratory, dining rooms, etc. All types of wards face south and have mutually isolated balconies for patients to rest. With ample sunlight and fresh air, it is one of the most modern sanatoriums in the country. Dr. Ding Huikang, the director of the sanatorium, recently took the Kang Lang Suo ship to Europe and the United States to study hospital management methods and medical conditions. Dr. Yan Fuqing has been specially invited to take over as director. Dr. Yan believes that if women giving birth naturally enter the hospital, the equipment will be better and the hygiene will be cleaner. There are many women giving birth naturally from middle-class families and above in the city. Therefore, an obstetrics department has been added to the sanatorium, and Dr. Wang Yihui has been invited to preside over obstetrics and gynecology. Dr. Wang has in-depth academic knowledge, rich experience, and a long-standing reputation, and can be considered a talented person. In addition, Dr. Lin Yuanying has been invited to provide services day and night to meet the needs. In addition, a tuberculosis department has been added to diagnose and treat tuberculosis in various stages using the latest methods. Dr. Qian Muhan, a lung disease expert and director of Chengzhong Hospital in Jiangwan, has been hired to preside over the diagnosis. Furthermore, Dr. Yan believes that diagnosis is the most important part of treating diseases, and has hired Dr. Soosgan, a German expert, to be in charge of the experimental diagnosis aspect.

Xu Zuoxun and Others Propose to Reduce Ferry Fares 137

Due to Rural Bankruptcy

Xu Zuoxun, Xin Shenzhai, Gao Jiyun, Hua Xiqing, and others, for the sake of alleviating the burden on the poor laborers in Pudong, suggested to the Pudong Fellow Villagers Association to reduce the price of city ferry tickets and add third and fourth class cabins, etc. The association had submitted a request to the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau, which approved that the matter was to be handled by the Xingye Trust Company, so it could not be done. Xu and others believe that the collapse of the rural areas and the decline of industry are at an extreme point. Witnessing the situation, they feel compassion. They found that the city-run cross-river ferry reduced fares in the morning and evening to facilitate poor laborers. Long-distance ferries are the same. Although it is not possible to reduce the price of city ferry tickets or add third and fourth class cabins, at a minimum, it is appropriate to add special morning and evening shifts for the poor. The time should follow the example of the cross-river ferry, from 5:00 AM to 7:00 AM every day, and from 5:00 PM to 7:00 PM in the afternoon. The fare for round trip should be 50% of the current second-class fare, and baggage tickets should be waived to show consideration and benefit the poor. A special written opinion has been prepared and submitted to your association for discussion at the fourth general membership meeting. Special contact has been made with the Xingye Trust Company to achieve the goal. Anxious for a response. It is reported that the Pudong Fellow Villagers Association has included it in the agenda and will discuss it at today's general meeting.

Ministry of Industry and Commerce Notifies Chambers of Commerce that Facial Powder Exported to the Dutch East Indies Must Be Certified 138

Should be Sent to the Inspection Bureau for Chemical Testing

The Ministry of Industry and Commerce notified the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce yesterday that, according to a report from the Consulate in Surabaya, the Dutch East Indies government intends to crack down on facial powder exported from China because it contains lead. The Shanghai and Guangzhou Commodity Inspection Bureaus were ordered to collect and test the powder and report. Now, according to the principle of voluntary inspection adopted by the bureau, it is proposed to submit a draft of quality rules for the certification of export facial powder and cosmetics. The Ministry has approved it as ten provisional measures for the certification of export facial powder by the Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, and ordered the commodity inspection bureaus to comply. In addition to distribution, the original report from the Consulate in Surabaya and the aforementioned measures are enclosed for your information. This notice is hereby given. Attached are ten certification measures. Article 1: Those who need a government inspection agency to certify that export facial powder and cosmetics do not contain lead may apply to the local commodity inspection bureau for chemical testing and certification. Article 2: Businesses or manufacturers engaged in the export of facial powder and cosmetics should fill out a registration application form to the inspection bureau when applying for chemical testing and certification for the first time. The registration application form should contain the following information: (1) Name and location of the business or name and address of the manufacturer; (2) Types and names of facial powder sold or manufactured, and their trademarks; (3) Estimated annual production quantity and export quantity of various powders; (4) Manufacturing methods and raw materials used; (5) Location of manufacturing and name and experience of the chief manufacturing technician, and their address. Article 3: For registered facial powder and cosmetics businesses or manufacturers, the inspection bureau may send personnel to inspect, supervise, or provide guidance at any time. Article 4: Those engaged in the export of facial powder and cosmetics should submit the name and address of the applicant, or the address of the business, the name of the facial powder, packaging style, quantity and weight, manufacturing instructions, export date, name of the carrying ship, destination, and the name or business of the consignee, on the application form for chemical testing and certification, five days before boxing and customs declaration, and pay the required fees to the inspection bureau for verification. Article 5: The inspection bureau will send personnel to select samples in the order of receipt of the application form for chemical testing and certification. The methods are as follows: (1) For the same type of goods, the quantity of powder sampled from each hundred boxes shall be determined by the inspection bureau, but the minimum amount shall be 250 cubic centimeters; (2) After the sample powder is obtained, the inspection bureau shall take the necessary amount for inspection, divide it into three bottles, seal it, and add a mark. One bottle shall be used for chemical testing, and the remaining two bottles shall be stored by the inspection bureau and the applicant, respectively. The storage period shall be one year each, and the remaining powder shall be returned on the spot; (3) After sampling, the inspection bureau shall issue a sampling voucher. Article 6: The order of chemical testing shall be based on the order of application. The procedure shall be completed within four days after sampling. Article 7: For export facial powder that has been certified by the inspection bureau to be free of lead, in addition to issuing a certificate, a certificate of conformity shall also be issued and affixed to the box. Article 8: For facial powder that has been certified by the inspection bureau but not exported, the original applicant may, within one year, apply to the inspection bureau for a free re-inspection once for legitimate reasons. Article 9: The chemical testing and certification of export facial powder is based on a unit of one thousand boxes. The chemical testing fee for each unit is 6 national currency, and if it is less than one unit, it is calculated as one unit. Article 10: These measures shall be implemented from the date of promulgation of the Ministry's order.

Notice Regarding the Export of Chinese Goods to Brazil 140

Must Be Certified by Local Chamber of Commerce

The Brazilian Consul General in Shanghai sent a letter to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce yesterday, stating: "I am writing to inform you that according to the customs regulations of our country, for all foreign merchants who import goods, the invoice must be accompanied by a declaration from the local chamber of commerce of the country concerned, stating the following: 'This is to certify that the prices listed on this invoice are consistent with the market prices of the goods in this port.' I would like to ask your chamber to inform the exporters that all invoices for goods imported into our country must first be sent to your chamber for stamping and the above declaration must be copied. If you agree to do so, I would be grateful."

The Pawnbroking Industry in This City Held a Spring Conference Yesterday 148

Datong News Agency reported that the Shanghai Pawnbroking Industry Association held a spring conference at 2:00 PM yesterday at the pawnbroking office in Wu Jia Nong, Hou Jia Qiao, Nanshi. More than 40 members of the industry attended, including Ji Hong Chuan Zuo Heng, Ding He Du Yunchu, Tong Yi Wu Qiutao, Shun Kang Hu Chunsheng, Yu Tai Fang Minfu, Qian Yi Qu Qiufang, De He Shen Boxin, Yi Chang Huang Yuanren, Guang Da Zhang Shengyao, Bao Kang Weng Zhitian, and Tong Yi Xing Mengqun. The chairman was Chuan Zuoheng and the recorder was Yu Langxi. The discussions included: (1) The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce issued a survey form on the prosperity and decline of business, ordering the industry to fill it out. It was decided to reprint the form and distribute it to the industry, two copies per pawnshop, to fill it out truthfully and submit it to the association for compilation. (2) The association's office was previously decided to be renovated at a general meeting. However, due to the economic downturn, the industry is afraid that it will be difficult to bear the construction cost. Therefore, the main resolution was to decide that since the office would not be renovated, the office should consider the situation and find ways to repair it. (3) Omitted. (4) Mr. Hu Chunsheng's letter stated that the pawn industry was prosperous last year, and the profits came from the pawn industry filling up with goods. Starting this year, the industry should unite as one, unify interest rates, and refuse to pawn strange costumes. The government should also stipulate the clothing system for men and women, and use domestically produced cloth and silk fabrics as the only raw materials in order to save the industry. It was decided that the industry should pay special attention to the spring inventory this year and not reduce prices too much to avoid losses. (5) Omitted. (6) In the French Concession, some members of the industry intend to shorten the maturity period to twelve months. How should this be handled? Please make a public decision. It was decided that the members of the industry in the French Concession should convene a meeting to decide on their own. According to Mr. Chuan Zuoheng, chairman of the association, to the Datong News Agency reporter, the pawnbroking industry's business situation last year was that 95% of the companies lost money. The reason for the loss was the impact of the severe drop in prices. The past two years have been the most severe period of price decline. The maturity period of the pawn industry was originally 18 months, and the clothes that were pledged two years ago also matured last year. Therefore, the heavy losses were inevitable. As for the old companies that closed their pawnshops last year, there were Taichang, Anding, Nanda, Yuansheng, and others. As for the concession, it belongs to the new companies, and the situation is not very clear. It is speculated that there are not a few companies that have stopped operating.

Yangtze River Rises Seven Feet in Three Days, Full Line Open 149

After the 6th of this month, the Yangtze River water level suddenly decreased, and between Hankou and Jiujiang, it was only 11 feet and 2 inches. Large ships were all suspended, and all Yangtze River ships were restricted in loading. In the past three days, the water level of the Yangtze River has increased rapidly due to the rising water level of the Xiang River, rising by more than 2 feet per day. The new record of the Yangtze River rising water level is seven feet and several inches in three days. Yesterday, Hankou reported that the water level between Jiujiang and Hankou has risen to 15 feet and 5 inches, and the water level between Wuhu and Jiujiang has risen to 18 feet. The restriction on loading at Jianghanguan has been lifted, and the ships grounded on the Xiaogushan side of the Yangtze River have been rescued due to the rising water level. The shipping companies in this city have agreed that from today onwards, the restrictions on the loading of cargo on Yangtze River ships have been lifted, and upstream and downstream shipping has been completely opened.

Ningbo Fellow Villagers Association Concerned About the People's Food in Their Hometown 150

Discussing Purchasing 50,000 Stones of Saigon Rice

Expediting Spring Relief and Agricultural Relief in Ningbo

Mr. Yu Qiaqing, the chairman of the Shanghai Ningbo Fellow Villagers Association, sighed that the drought disaster in the counties of Ningbo last year was extremely serious. The Civil Affairs Department investigated the disaster situation and did not include the counties in the emergency winter relief. In fact, at the end of winter and the beginning of spring, farmers have no food to last overnight. Therefore, they are extremely concerned about the people's food in their hometown. A meeting of the committee was convened to discuss jointly raising funds to purchase 50,000 stones of Saigon rice to expedite spring relief and agricultural relief to relieve the suffering. It is reported that the association has sent a special letter to the Quan Zhe Relief Association to obtain a tax-free passport to facilitate the process. The letter states: "I am writing to inform you that the drought ravaged the land last year, and the severity of the disaster was unprecedented. The disaster situation in the old Ningbo prefectures, such as Yin, Ci, Zhen, Feng, Ding, and Xiang counties, is no different from that of the counties in western Zhejiang. However, the Civil Affairs Department's investigation of the disaster situation did not include the counties in the emergency winter relief. Perhaps it is because the silkworm industry in western Zhejiang has been in poor harvest for many years and the price of silk has plummeted, coupled with the drought disaster, which is even more painful in comparison, resulting in the exclusion of Ningbo. It is not known that Ningbo is not a rice-producing area, and even in a year of good harvest, it is not enough to be self-sufficient. In addition, the people lack food in the event of a major disaster. At the end of winter and the beginning of spring, farmers have no food to last overnight. In the blink of an eye, they will be engaged in morning farming. The situation is unimaginable at a time when the new and old crops are not connected. Our colleagues in the association have repeatedly met and discussed and plan to purchase 50,000 stones of Saigon rice to expedite spring relief and agricultural relief to relieve the suffering. In addition to the county governments and relief sub-associations doing their best to raise funds, the shortfall will be raised by our association from the fellow villagers in Shanghai. Therefore, we are writing to ask your association to transfer the request to the Relief Committee to transfer it to the Ministry of Finance to issue a tax-free passport for 50,000 stones to facilitate relief. We are anxiously awaiting your reply."

Workers at Tianzhang Paper Mill Strike 151

Due to Unequal Treatment Between the East and West Factories by the Employer

And the Dismissal of More Than Ten Members of the Labor Union

The Tianzhang Paper East Factory in Lujiazui, Pudong, employs more than 100 workers. Last year, the workers repeatedly requested the Party and government authorities through the Fifth District Paper Workers Union to mediate because the factory could not provide the same treatment as the West Factory of the company, paying bonuses for annual paper. It has been nearly a year and has not been resolved. Recently, it has been learned that at the end of this year, the staff and tea servants of the East Factory have received bonuses, while the workers who have worked hard day and night have received nothing, which has caused deep resentment between labor and capital. On the 10th of this month, the workers expressed dissatisfaction with the factory's delay in paying wages for six days, which caused a slowdown strike. The labor union persuaded the workers to retreat, and Li, the captain of the third squadron of the local police, took on the role of mediation. Both parties unconditionally resumed work. Unexpectedly, after the incident, the factory suddenly dismissed eleven people, including Jin Changfa, the director of the labor union, and Chen Lizhi, a member, on the pretext that the workers went on strike. More than 20 police officers were deployed inside and outside the factory, as if facing a great enemy. The labor union sent personnel to negotiate, but to no avail. As a result, all the workers went on strike together. After the Fifth District Paper Workers Union reported the incident, in addition to sending personnel to comfort the workers and maintain order, it has reported to the Party and government authorities and the General Labor Union for verification.

Summary of Public and Private Construction in the Shanghai International Settlement Last Month 152

According to the report by the Chief of Works of the Public Works Department of the Shanghai Municipal Council, in January, among the public works projects, two new school buildings, namely the Hanbury Girls' School and the Chinese Girls' Elementary School, were completed and handed over for use. The interior decoration of the new Fuzhou Road Central Police Station building is still in progress, and drainage pipes have been installed in the courtyard. The East Hongkou Vegetable Market is half completed. The framework of the new bridge on Dinghai Road has been installed, but the project has been slightly delayed due to the severe cold.

In terms of private construction, there are 290 projects currently underway. 166 construction blueprints were submitted, 85 of which were approved. The Public Works Department assessed the value of 58 properties and inspected 4,601 residences.

The Public Works Department's cleaning work included sweeping 1,616 tons of dust and debris from the roads, clearing 2,167 tons of materials from the ditches, using 410,400 gallons of water for sprinkling roads, and 2,186,400 gallons of water for washing roads. 4,818 tons of household garbage were transported by trucks and handcarts for landfill, and 16,586 tons were transported by contractors by boat. A total of 7,198 tons of garbage and sweepings were sent to the two incinerators for incineration.

Condition of Milk Supply in the Shanghai International Settlement

The supply of fresh milk and cheese in the Shanghai International Settlement comes from 2,162 yellow cattle, 206 water buffalo, and 118 goats. There are 28 dairy farms, 10 of which have "Grade A" licenses and 17 of which have "Grade B" licenses. The average daily milk production in the morning is 30,380 pounds, an increase of 17% compared to the previous year.

The cattle at each farm are regularly inspected by the Municipal Council's veterinarians. The cattle at Grade B farms are examined individually every six months, and the cattle at Grade A farms are examined individually every three months, with temporary inspections in addition. The fresh meat in the Public Settlement comes from Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Shandong, and Anhui provinces. The slaughtering places include the Municipal Council's large slaughterhouse, the Municipal Council's pig slaughterhouse, and four private pig slaughterhouses. Nowadays, the slaughtering of cattle, sheep, and pigs all adopts new humane methods, with excellent results. Butchers and meat vendors initially strongly opposed the new methods, but their opposition has gradually subsided.

Inspection Report of the China Land Reclamation Bank

The special issuance preparation inspection report of the China Land Reclamation Bank states that the issuance treasury and business treasury of the China Land Reclamation Bank have always been completely separated. According to the regulations of the bank's articles of association, cash reserves are above 70%, and guarantee reserves are below 30%. On the 16th of this month, the results of the inspection by accountant Wang Zikang, together with Xu Jimiao and Xu Busun, representatives of the board of directors and supervisors, are as follows: the total amount of exchange coupons issued is 6.89 million silver dollars, and the total amount of exchange coupon reserve funds is 6.89 million silver dollars, including cash reserves of 5,123,000 silver dollars and guarantee reserves of 1,767,000 silver dollars. According to the investigation, the cash reserve accounts for slightly more than 74%, and the guarantee reserve accounts for slightly less than 26%. This is a special report. February 16, 1935.

Recent News from the South Shanghai Rent Reduction Association

Representatives of Various Lane Neighborhoods Hold a Joint Meeting

The South Shanghai Rent Reduction Committee has been working practically since it suspended its meetings last November, focusing on mediation between members. To date, after three months, the rent reduction for 80% of the households registered with the committee has been resolved. Therefore, the committee believes that the rent reduction work has largely come to an end. However, the landlord of Anhe Company on Luxiang Road, Ji畝地, sent a letter stating that if rent can be paid in advance, they will consider reducing it accordingly. The committee notified the tenants to pay rent in advance, but the landlord has not yet made a firm statement, and the tenants are impatient. Therefore, at 2 pm the day before yesterday, a joint meeting of representatives of various lane neighborhoods was held in the committee's auditorium. More than 40 people attended, including Shen Xinwu from the Minguo Road Branch, Chen Yuanling from the Chongde Lane Branch, Gu Xiayun from the Chengzhi Lane Branch, Zhang Binghua from the Pudong Branch, and Wang Zhangfei from the Nanren'an Lane Branch. Sun Nai was elected chairman, and Ni Yiguan recorded the minutes. The following resolutions were made: (1) The landlord of Yuyuan Lane in Zhabei High-handedly brought a lawsuit claiming rent arrears. After the entire lane petitioned, it was approved to present reasons and handle the case accordingly. (Resolution) File a lawsuit according to law. Before the lawsuit is resolved, the rent will be temporarily deposited in the bank. (2) Dr. Zhang Xingruo, a famous doctor on Pingqiao Road, owns property in the Nanshi area. After the committee sent a letter, Zhang Shoulian's rent of 110 yuan per month was involved in a lawsuit and was ordered to be reduced by 20 yuan per month from February 1933. How should this be expressed? (Resolution) In addition to sending a letter of thanks, publish an announcement praising his benevolence. (3) After the committee sent a letter to Anhe Company on Luxiang Road, ordering a 40% rent reduction, the company asked for rent to be paid in advance during the lunar New Year, saying they would consider reducing it accordingly. The committee has notified the tenants to pay rent in advance, but the landlord has not yet made a statement. How should this be handled? (Resolution) Send another letter urging them. If there is no definite reply, the rent will be stored in the bank at a 40% reduction. (4) Several thousand households have registered with the committee and have had their rent reduced. How should landlords and tenants cooperate in practice? (Resolution) Organize a Citizens' Happiness Mutual Aid Association, with enthusiastic representatives as initiators. [Remainder omitted.] The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Scota Cup Semi-Finals, Donghua to Play Rucks Today 153

3 PM at Shenyuan Football Field

Yesterday, French Business Beat Chinese Police 9-0

In yesterday's Scota Cup semi-final, French Business defeated Chinese Police 9-0, securing a spot in the final. The other semi-final, between Donghua and Rucks, is scheduled for 3 PM today at Shenyuan, to determine who will face French Business in the final. Both Donghua and Rucks have plenty of talent and strength. Donghua is undefeated in the First Division League. While Rucks may not be as strong as Donghua, it is the strongest of the Western teams and a formidable opponent for Donghua. Their encounter is sure to be intensely competitive. Today's schedule is as follows:

Donghua vs. Rucks Scota Cup Shenyuan Li Nuosi

(Linesmen Chang Shen Huichun Peel)

Western Police vs. Jewish Team First Division Racecourse Na Aituo

Western Business vs. English News First Division Racecourse Bo Tuo

Donghua announces that Donghua will play Rucks in the Scota Cup at Shenyuan today. Donghua's lineup is as follows:

Lu Zhongen Li Ning Guan Xun'an Gu Shangxiang Feng Yunyou Ding Zhaocheng Wan Xianghua Li Yichen Dai Linjing Chen Jiaqiu Jia Youliang

In yesterday's Scota Cup semi-final match between French Business and Chinese Police, held in Yiwei, French Business eliminated Chinese Police 9-0 to secure a spot in the final, where they will face the winner of today's Donghua-Rucks match.

Strength Ultimately Inferior

After eliminating Western Business with a 1-0 victory, the Chinese Police surprised everyone. In Beijing during the New Year, they defeated Jinghua 4-1. However, their strength was ultimately much inferior to that of French Business, and there was nothing they could do about it. However, given time, they may become something special.

Five International Players

French Business added one international player to their forward line yesterday, namely Kelasha. As a result, their strength increased significantly, and their attack was particularly fierce. If they face Donghua in the final, it will be a spectacle to behold. Yesterday, French Business had a total of five international players: Kelasha, Fafanxiao, Lemidi, Mashan'er, and Huate. It is no wonder that Chinese Police were defeated.

Stalemate Lasted Twenty Minutes

The two sides were evenly matched for twenty minutes. Chinese Police were in high spirits and had good leg strength. They ran around tirelessly and even managed to attack the French Business goal. For a time, French Business seemed helpless. Chinese Police kicked off, and French Business's Qinsheng dribbled straight in. Miao Huaguo cleared the ball. Wu Xiquan attacked along the wing several times, but with little success due to his lack of strength. French Business gradually gained the upper hand, but Chinese Police built a strong defense, and French Business could not cross the line. They held out until the twentieth minute when Baoxiu Tuo angled a shot, breaking the Chinese Police's iron gate.

First Half Four to Zero

After Baoxiu Tuo's goal, the situation changed completely. After Dong Zhaobin's free kick from outside the penalty line failed, Lemidi flew in and Baoxiu Tuo headed in another goal. Yin Xingsheng picked it up and lost it again. Xiao Dong pushed it in lightly, making it three to zero. Fafanxiao also scored. At halftime, French Business led 4-0.

Second Half Five to Zero

As a result, the Chinese Police completely collapsed. In the first minute of the second half, Kelasha launched an attack. The ball bounced off the goal and did not go in. Fafanxiao was tripped, and Lemidi scored a penalty, making it 5-0. The French Police were now at the mercy of French Business, and many mistakes were made. Fafanxiao made a great effort to score the sixth goal, Kelasha the seventh, Qinsheng the eighth, and Fafanxiao scored the final ninth goal. The Chinese Police failed to score, and their lack of strength was a matter of fate.

Ministry of Education Statistics on the Current Situation of National Social Education 160

The Ministry of Education's statistics on the general situation of national social education:

Nineteen key points are summarized as follows: (1) The number of national social education institutions has increased from more than 10,000 to more than 78,000 in the past four years. (2) Social education funding has increased from more than 3.6 million yuan to more than 14 million yuan. (3) The number of social education institution staff has increased from more than 14,000 to more than 131,000 in the past four years. (4) The number of students and visitors to social education institutions has increased from more than 219,000 to more than 1.252 million in the past four years. (5) The number of literacy and writing services for the public has increased by more than 3,000, and the number of public schools, public newspaper reading rooms, and literacy classes has increased by more than 1,000. (6) The most increased social education funding is the Public Education Center, which has increased by more than 340,000 yuan, and public schools and orphan and poor children's education and care homes have increased by more than 200,000 yuan. (7) The social education institution staff that has increased the most is the public school, which has increased by more than 12,000 people, the public literacy and writing service has increased by more than 2,000 people, and the public newspaper reading room and the phonetic symbol training institute have increased by more than 1,000 people. (8) The school-style social education institutions that have increased the most in participation and student numbers are the public school, which has increased by more than 117,000 people, the public literacy class, which has increased by more than 23,000 people, and the phonetic symbol training institute, which has increased by more than 18,000 people. (9) The number of public education personnel training institutions has increased by 10. (10) The average cost per graduate of each public school is 5 yuan and 76 cents, and the average number of teachers and students per public school is 29. (11) The province with the largest increase in social education institutions is Hebei, with an increase of 3,462. (12) The province with the largest increase in social education funding is Hebei, with an increase of more than 300,000 yuan, and Shandong, Henan, Fujian, and Beiping have also increased by more than 200,000 yuan. (13) The province with the largest increase in social education institution staff is Hebei, with an increase of 8,519 people, and Yunnan and Henan have each increased by more than 3,000 people. (14) The province with the largest increase in the number of students and visitors to social education institutions is Hebei, with more than 92,000 people, and Yunnan, with more than 31,000 people. (15) Among the public schools that have increased more than before, Hebei has increased by more than 2,000 schools, Chahar Province has increased by 18 supplementary schools, Guangdong has increased by 58 public education centers, and Henan has increased by 27 libraries. (16) The highest cost per graduate of each public school is Shanghai, with 22 yuan and 95 cents, and the lowest is Weihaiwei, with 67 cents. (17) The provinces with social education funding budgets that have reached the standards ordered by the national government in the 20th year are Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Fujian, Beijing, Shanghai, and Weihaiwei, in the 21st year, there are Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Fujian, Qingdao, and Weihaiwei, and in the 22nd year, there are Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Fujian, Beijing, Qingdao, and Weihaiwei. (18) The county and city social education funding budgets that have reached the standards prescribed by the national government in the 20th year are Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Rehe, in the 21st year, there are Jiangsu, Suiyuan, Guizhou, Shaanxi, and Rehe, and in the 22nd year, there are Ningxia, Yunnan, Guangxi, Zhejiang, Shaanxi, and Jiangsu. (19) The provinces and cities with the highest average social education funding burden per person per year are Beiping, with 6 jiao, 3 fen, and 9 li, and the lowest is Xikang, with 1 li. The national average burden is 6 fen and 3 li.

Director Pan's Opinions on Ten Scholars' Declarations 167

Approving the Principle of the Declaration and Proposing Basic Work

The First Step of Enlightenment Should Start with Education

Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau, gave a speech at the China Arts and Crafts Society at 2:30 PM yesterday, attended by more than 500 teachers and staff from various schools. The topic was "The Enlightenment Movement of Chinese-Based Cultural Construction." In addition to explaining in detail the declaration of Chinese-based cultural construction issued by the Ten Professors, he also contributed to the basic work of cultural construction. The speech was very long, and the following is an excerpt of the main points: Pan first expressed his approval of the principles of the Ten Declarations, and then said that the basic work to be done to break the current state of ignorance and confusion is to do the first step of work, and then the second step of work can be done. If the first step of enlightenment work is not done, it is impossible to build a culture. Those who are responsible for this enlightenment work are first of all people in the education field. Culture is the moderation of all lifestyles and life forms of human beings. It is all-encompassing and all-purpose. Culture cannot be built by a few people, especially not by one or two people. Of course, it first depends on the foresight and consciousness of the promoters, and then on the propaganda of the afterthought and consciousness, but most people must be able to imitate this way of life before it can be done to build a culture. The so-called culture, "wen" is civilization, and "hua" is change and dissolution. To change and deepen to tend towards civilization is culture. Therefore, culture is civilization. However, "hua" must be universal. If it is not universal, it cannot be considered "hua." Therefore, the first step in building a culture is to enable most people to receive this lifestyle and do it according to this lifestyle, which must rely on the enlightenment movement. The so-called enlightenment, in other words, is the popularization of education movement. Cultural construction must start with education. Without education, it is impossible to talk about cultural construction. The meaning of education is divided into two aspects: one is the guidance of thought, so that spiritual life is happy, and the other is the training of skills, so that material life progresses. The former is literacy education, and the latter is production education. Only when the two can be taken care of without being biased can they be considered complete education. Only by popularizing this kind of education can people be able to receive new lifestyles. Therefore, the foundation of the enlightenment movement for cultural construction is the education field.

Special Feature

What University Graduates Should Know When Serving in the Banking Industry 170

(2) Tang Shoumin

(2) Serve Loyally: You should work for the organization, not for individuals. You should consider serving the organization as a lifelong career. Be loyal and persevere. Avoid restlessness, indecision, or changing your mind frequently. The purpose of this bank hiring you is to cultivate sound banking talent. If, after being trained, you immediately move to other fields, it will discourage various organizations, businesses, and merchants in society from wanting to employ university graduates. I hope you will not have such thoughts. If you unfortunately harbor such ideas, you should realize this as soon as possible.

(3) Responsibility: You all come from universities or specialized colleges, and you certainly understand the importance of responsibility. This means not shirking responsibility beforehand and not evading it afterward. Do what you say, and speak after you have done it. All assigned tasks should be handled responsibly and completed quickly within the shortest possible time.

(4) Cooperation: Since you have resolved to serve here, you must not only be responsible and patient but also possess a spirit of cooperation. Especially in larger organizations, you should maximize this spirit. For example, if there are errors in the work of the lending department, the accounting department should be attentive and carefully check the calculations. When errors are found, everyone should work together, without being divisive, to avoid losses to the entire organization.

(5) Treat People with Humility and Sincerity: Commercial firms sell goods, while financial institutions do not sell silver dollars or banknotes. What they sell is "service." You should treat customers with diligence and courtesy. Ordinary people generally feel that bank employees consider themselves to be of a high status, arrogant and conceited. Especially towards some of the older, larger banks, many people are afraid to even enter. Although they have savings, they are afraid to deposit them. This bad habit greatly affects the banks. Please pay special attention to this.

(6) Diligent and Careful Service: Modern banks should pay the most attention to providing thorough service to customers, especially "counter service." This bank has a similar position to major banks. As long as our service is good, not arrogant, and not deceptive, we can surpass others. Speak truthfully, and treat people sincerely. When I was the Deputy Manager of the Shanghai Bank, I promoted an idea to supervise the employees, which was that "the Deputy Manager should also sit at the counter." As a result, everyone provided particularly diligent service and had no arrogance. At that time, we were very popular with customers and praised by society. It is best for the cashier to chat with customers while paying, to dispel their boredom and create a good impression. If you treat people with arrogance, no matter how much you advertise, it will be useless.

(7) Engage in Research: Service should not come at the expense of reading. In your spare time, read books on banking to supplement your knowledge, increase your experience, and develop your abilities. For all unfamiliar banking practices, you should engage in research and ask experienced individuals for guidance. Be humble and avoid being too subjective or overly complacent. Publish your research findings in communications from time to time.

(8) Resist Assimilation: Everyone has their own thoughts and strengths. If you can contribute these strengths as much as possible, the organization will surely thrive. I welcome your good suggestions, and I will adopt them within the possible scope. The worst thing is not having good suggestions yourself while being suspicious and slandering the suggestions of others. As a result, no one speaks up, no one wants to seek progress and development for the entire organization, and everyone becomes corrupt and lifeless. If there are people with these habits, you should assimilate them, not be assimilated by them.

Furthermore, I would like to take this opportunity to talk about the salary issue for employees in this bank. In society, many organizations and businesses, except for the post office and customs, do not treat their employees as well as banks. If you can fully demonstrate your abilities, you can increase your salary at any time. In the past, it was customary for branch managers and deputy managers to request salary increases for their colleagues at the end of each year. This was done for both diligent and capable employees and for those who were lazy and incompetent. For example, if a branch had 30 employees, more than 20 could be promoted, and the remaining few would also be promoted out of consideration for their feelings. As a result, performance evaluations were essentially meaningless, increasing expenses each year and reducing the efficiency of hard-working employees. This is regrettable. Therefore, last year, I re-evaluated the salaries of all employees, both low and high. From now on, if a supervisor says that an employee is performing well, that employee can be given a salary increase at any time. "Increases every day, increases every moment," depend entirely on your abilities and hard work as the standard for promotion and the method for increasing salaries. As for bonuses, in the past, they were distributed according to salary regardless of performance. This method essentially defeats the purpose of rewards. In the future, we will implement rewards based on merit. Those with excellent service can receive more, while those with poor evaluations, those with faults, or those with excessive leave may not receive any at all.

Another point you should understand is that when the organization establishes new branches or transfers personnel, you must comply with the transfers, regardless of the distance. After being transferred to various places, you will have the opportunity to understand the financial and economic conditions of different regions, which will help you become national financial talents. This is what I very much hope for.

Finally, you all have different areas of expertise, such as accounting, economics, agriculture, textiles, etc. Those who specialize in accounting have been assigned to the Audit Department. In the near future, we will add a training class for accountants. The goal is to ensure that you fully understand everything "from vouchers to final accounts." After training, you will be assigned to various branches to work as accountants, while the original accounting staff will be transferred back to the head office to work in auditing. Those assigned to the business department will also use a practical training method, where the original operators will stand beside you and provide guidance. After you become proficient, the original staff will be transferred. The overall goal is to improve the abilities of all employees, so that they can be applied everywhere. Those with a background in textile schools can be sent to various textile factories for practical training. It is hoped that all other specialists will focus on their work. One more thing to remember is to admit and correct your mistakes and not be affected by negative assimilation. Strive forward, so as not to disappoint the original intention of cultivating you all. (End)

Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

Speaking Out for Many Unfortunate Children 171

— Hongxia

When we walk through the streets and alleys, we can see many children with runny noses and wearing tattered clothes, jumping, running, and playing.

When a child carrying a schoolbag walks past excitedly, they will stare with envy, seeming to harbor resentment and sigh deeply.

Under the scorching sun or in the freezing cold, many school-age children are selling fried dough sticks, melon seeds, and peanuts, their cries piercing the hearts of people, leaving a bitter feeling.

Are they all born with a miserable fate? Among them, many hope to study and seek knowledge. However, the social environment and the pressures of life do not allow them to develop their potential.

This year is the Year of the Child. It is hoped that people of ambition in the country will quickly find ways to save these poor, unfortunate children. Perhaps the core members who will save the country in the future will be among this group of children!

Clever and Studious Children in Ancient Times 172

— Dazhai

Pei Xiu of the Jin Dynasty studied diligently and was able to write at the age of eight. A friend praised him, saying, "Pei Xiu will be a leader of outstanding talents." A leader is someone extraordinary. Children, if you aspire to be an extraordinary person and do extraordinary things in the future, you must work hard from a young age, lest you grieve when you are old.

Xu Ling of the Southern and Northern Dynasties loved reading historical records from a young age. Like Pei Xiu, he was able to write at the age of eight. By the age of thirteen, he was familiar with Lao Tzu and Zhuangzi. He read a lot and memorized numerous "classics," so his writing almost always quoted "classics." This style was called Six Dynasties literature. Together with Yu Xin, they were known as the Xu-Yu style, which has been passed down to this day. Now, times are different, and children do not necessarily need to seek "classics" in ancient books. However, how much common sense do you have in your heart? Hurry up and work hard!

Li He of the Tang Dynasty was able to write poetry at the age of seven. At that time, two great writers, Han Yu and Huangfu Shi, did not believe this, thinking, how could a seven-year-old child be a "poet"? They suspected that someone was writing for him and pretending. The two went to Li He's house to see him write poetry in person. Li He took up a pen and immediately composed a poem titled "High Carriage Passes By." Han Yu and Huangfu Shi were greatly surprised and said it was "rare and valuable." Children, do people praise your work when they see it? If not, you must practice diligently, and you will gradually improve. If you don't do this, time will pass easily, and you will easily transform from a child into an adult with still incoherent sentences and numerous typos. Wouldn't you be laughed at? Judge by the small, so don't miss this "golden age."

— Cheng Lilai
